74→// TODO(negz): Stop using a package scoped logger. At the time of writing we're\n    75→// creating an etcd client for each CRD. We need to pass each etcd client a\n    76→// logger or each client will create its own, which comes with a significant\n    77→// memory cost (around 20% of the API server's memory when hundreds of CRDs are\n    78→// present). The correct fix here is to not create a client per CRD.   127→}\n   128→\n   129→// atomic error acts as a cache for atomically store an error\n   130→// the error is only updated if the timestamp is more recent than\n   131→// current stored error.\n   132→type atomicLastError struct {\n   133→\tmu        sync.RWMutex\n   134→\terr       error\n   135→\ttimestamp time.Time\n   136→}\n   137→\n   138→func (a *atomicLastError) Store(err error, t time.Time) {\n   139→\ta.mu.Lock()\n   140→\tdefer a.mu.Unlock()\n   141→\tif a.timestamp.IsZero() || a.timestamp.Before(t) {\n   142→\t\ta.err = err\n   143→\t\ta.timestamp = t\n   144→\t}\n   145→}\n   146→\n   147→func (a *atomicLastError) Load() error {\n   148→\ta.mu.RLock()\n   149→\tdefer a.mu.RUnlock()\n   150→\treturn a.err\n   151→}\n   152→\n   153→func newETCD3Check(c storagebackend.Config, timeout time.Duration, stopCh <-chan struct{}) (func() error, error) {\n   154→\t// constructing the etcd v3 client blocks and times out if etcd is not available.\n   155→\t// retry in a loop in the background until we successfully create the client, storing the client or error encountered\n   156→\n   157→\tlock := sync.RWMutex{}\n   158→\tvar prober *etcd3ProberMonitor\n   159→\tclientErr := fmt.Errorf(\"etcd client connection not yet established\")\n   160→\n   161→\tgo wait.PollImmediateUntil(time.Second, func() (bool, error) {\n   162→\t\tlock.Lock()\n   163→\t\tdefer lock.Unlock()\n   164→\t\tnewProber, err := newETCD3ProberMonitor(c)\n   165→\t\t// Ensure that server is already not shutting down.\n   166→\t\tselect {\n   167→\t\tcase <-stopCh:\n   168→\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   169→\t\t\t\tnewProber.Close()\n   170→\t\t\t}\n   171→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   172→\t\tdefault:\n   173→\t\t}\n   174→\t\tif err != nil {\n   175→\t\t\tclientErr = err\n   176→\t\t\treturn false, nil\n   177→\t\t}\n   178→\t\tprober = newProber\n   179→\t\tclientErr = nil\n   180→\t\treturn true, nil\n   181→\t}, stopCh)\n   182→\n   183→\t// Close the client on shutdown.\n   184→\tgo func() {\n   185→\t\tdefer utilruntime.HandleCrash()\n   186→\t\t<-stopCh\n   187→\n   188→\t\tlock.Lock()\n   189→\t\tdefer lock.Unlock()\n   190→\t\tif prober != nil {\n   191→\t\t\tprober.Close()\n   192→\t\t\tclientErr = fmt.Errorf(\"server is shutting down\")\n   193→\t\t}\n   194→\t}()\n   195→\n   196→\t// limit to a request every half of the configured timeout with a maximum burst of one\n   197→\t// rate limited requests will receive the last request sent error (note: not the last received response)\n   198→\tlimiter := rate.NewLimiter(rate.Every(timeout/2), 1)\n   199→\t// initial state is the clientErr\n   200→\tlastError := &atomicLastError{err: fmt.Errorf(\"etcd client connection not yet established\")}\n   201→\n   202→\treturn func() error {\n   203→\t\t// Given that client is closed on shutdown we hold the lock for\n   204→\t\t// the entire period of healthcheck call to ensure that client will\n   205→\t\t// not be closed during healthcheck.\n   206→\t\t// Given that healthchecks has a 2s timeout, worst case of blocking\n   207→\t\t// shutdown for additional 2s seems acceptable.\n   208→\t\tlock.RLock()\n   209→\t\tdefer lock.RUnlock()\n   210→\n   211→\t\tif clientErr != nil {\n   212→\t\t\treturn clientErr\n   213→\t\t}\n   214→\t\tif limiter.Allow() == false {\n   215→\t\t\treturn lastError.Load()\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), timeout)\n   218→\t\tdefer cancel()\n   219→\t\tnow := time.Now()\n   220→\t\terr := prober.Probe(ctx)\n   221→\t\tlastError.Store(err, now)\n   222→\t\treturn err\n   223→\t}, nil\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→func newETCD3ProberMonitor(c storagebackend.Config) (*etcd3ProberMonitor, 373→)\n   374→\n   375→// startCompactorOnce start one compactor per transport. If the interval get smaller on repeated calls, the\n   376→// compactor is replaced. A destroy func is returned. If all destroy funcs with the same transport are called,\n   377→// the compactor is stopped.\n   378→func startCompactorOnce(c storagebackend.TransportConfig, interval time.Duration) (func(), error) {\n   379→\tcompactorsMu.Lock()\n   380→\tdefer compactorsMu.Unlock()\n   381→\n   382→\tif interval == 0 {\n   383→\t\t// short circuit, if the compaction request from apiserver is disabled\n   384→\t\treturn func() {}, nil\n   385→\t}\n   386→\tkey := fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", c) // gives: {[server1 server2] keyFile certFile caFile}\n   387→\tif compactor, foundBefore := compactors[key];   405→\n   406→\t\tcompactor.interval = interval\n   407→\t\tcompactor.cancel = cancel\n   408→\t\tcompactor.client = compactorClient\n   409→\n   410→\t\tetcd3.StartCompactor(ctx, compactorClient, interval)\n   411→\t}\n   412→\n   413→\tcompactors[key].refs++\n   414→\n   415→\treturn func() {\n   416→\t\tcompactorsMu.Lock()\n   417→\t\tdefer compactorsMu.Unlock()\n   418→\n   419→\t\tcompactor := compactors[key]\n   420→\t\tcompactor.refs--\n   421→\t\tif compactor.refs == 0 {\n   422→\t\t\tcompactor.cancel()\n   423→\t\t\tcompactor.client.Close()\n   424→\t\t\tdelete(compactors, key)\n   425→\t\t}\n   426→\t}, nil\n   427→}\n   428→\n   429→func newETCD3Storage(c storagebackend.ConfigForResource, newFunc, newListFunc func() runtime.Object, 474→func startDBSizeMonitorPerEndpoint(client *clientv3.Client, interval time.Duration) (func(), error) {\n   475→\tif interval == 0 {\n   476→\t\treturn func() {}, nil\n   477→\t}\n the timeout for failing to establish a connection.\n\t// It is set to 20 seconds as times shorter than that will cause TLS connections to fail\n\t// on heavily loaded arm64 CPUs (issue #64649)\n\tdialTimeout = 20 * time.Second\n\n\tdbMetricsMonitorJitter = 0.5\n)\n\n// TODO(negz): Stop using a package scoped logger. At the time of writing we're\n// creating an etcd client for each CRD. We need to pass each etcd client a\n// logger or each client will create its own, which comes with a significant\n// memory cost (around 20% of the API server's memory when hundreds of CRDs are\n// present). The correct fix here is to not create a client per CRD. See\n// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/111476 for more.\nvar etcd3ClientLogger *zap.Logger\n\nfunc init() {\n\t// grpcprom auto-registers (via an init function) their client metrics, since we are opting out of\n\t// using the global prometheus registry and using our own wrapped global registry,\n\t// we need to explicitly register these metrics to our global registry here.\n\t// For reference: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/pull/81387\n\tlegacyregistry.RawMustRegister(grpcprom.DefaultClientMetrics)\n\tdbMetricsMonitors = make(map[string]struct{})\n\n\tl, err := logutil.CreateDefaultZapLogger(etcdClientDebugLevel())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tl = zap.NewNop()\n\t}\n\tetcd3ClientLogger = l.Named(\"etcd-client\")\n}\n\n// etcdClientDebugLevel translates ETCD_CLIENT_DEBUG into zap log level.\n// NOTE(negz): This is a copy of a private etcd client function:\n// https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/blob/v3.5.4/client/v3/logger.go#L47\nfunc etcdClientDebugLevel() zapcore.Level {\n\tenvLevel := os.Getenv(\"ETCD_CLIENT_DEBUG\")\n\tif envLevel == \"\" || envLevel == \"true\" {\n\t\treturn zapcore.InfoLevel\n\t}\n\tvar l zapcore.Level\n\tif err := l.Set(envLevel); err == nil {\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"Deprecated env ETCD_CLIENT_DEBUG value. is more recent than\n// current stored error.\ntype atomicLastError struct {\n\tmu        sync.RWMutex\n\terr       error\n\ttimestamp time.Time\n}\n\nfunc (a *atomicLastError) Store(err error, t time.Time) {\n\ta.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer a.mu.Unlock()\n\tif a.timestamp.IsZero() || a.timestamp.Before(t) {\n\t\ta.err = err\n\t\ta.timestamp = t\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (a *atomicLastError) Load() error {\n\ta.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer a.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn a.err\n}\n\nfunc newETCD3Check(c storagebackend.Config, timeout time.Duration, stopCh <-chan struct{}) (func() error, error) {\n\t// constructing the etcd v3 client blocks and times out if etcd is not available.\n\t// retry in a loop in the background until we successfully create the client, storing the client or error encountered\n\n\tlock := sync.RWMutex{}\n\tvar prober *etcd3ProberMonitor\n\tclientErr := fmt.Errorf(\"etcd client connection not yet established\")\n\n\tgo wait.PollImmediateUntil(time.Second, func() (bool, error) nil {\n\t\t\t\tnewProber.Close()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tclientErr = err\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tprober = newProber\n\t\tclientErr = nil\n\t\treturn true, nil\n\t}, stopCh)\n\n\t// Close the client on shutdown.\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tdefer utilruntime.HandleCrash()\n\t\t<-stopCh\n\n\t\tlock.Lock()\n\t\tdefer lock.Unlock()\n\t\tif prober != nil {\n\t\t\tprober.Close()\n\t\t\tclientErr = fmt.Errorf(\"server is shutting down\")\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\t// limit to a request every half of the configured timeout with a maximum burst of one\n\t// rate limited requests will receive the last request sent error (note: not the last received response)\n\tlimiter := rate.NewLimiter(rate.Every(timeout/2), 1)\n\t// initial state is the clientErr\n\tlastError := &atomicLastError{err: fmt.Errorf(\"etcd client connection not yet established\")}\n\n\treturn func() error {\n\t\t// Given that client is closed on shutdown we hold the lock for\n\t\t// the entire period of healthcheck call to ensure that client will\n\t\t// not be closed during healthcheck.\n\t\t// Given that healthchecks has a 2s timeout, worst case of blocking\n\t\t// shutdown for additional 2s seems acceptable.\n\t\tlock.RLock()\n\t\tdefer lock.RUnlock()\n\n\t\tif clientErr != nil {\n\t\t\treturn clientErr\n\t\t}\n\t\tif limiter.Allow() == false {\n\t\t\treturn lastError.Load()\n\t\t}\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t\tnow := time.Now()\n\t\terr := prober.Probe(ctx)\n\t\tlastError.Store(err, now)\n\t\treturn err\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc newETCD3ProberMonitor(c storagebackend.Config) (*etcd3ProberMonitor, error) {\n\tclient, err := For instance, cross\n\t// datacenter deployment may require longer election timeout of 10-second.\n\t// If true, local node does not need wait up to 10-second. Instead,\n\t// forwards its election ticks to 8-second, and have only 2-second left\n\t// before leader election.\n\t//\n\t// Major assumptions are that:\n\t//  - cluster has no active leader thus advancing ticks enables faster\n\t//    leader election, or\n\t//  - cluster already has an established leader, and rejoining follower\n\t//    is likely to receive heartbeats from the leader after tick advance\n\t//    and before election timeout.\n\t//\n\t// However, when network from leader to rejoining follower is congested,\n\t// and the follower does not receive leader heartbeat within left election\n\t// ticks, disruptive election has to happen thus affecting cluster\n\t// availabilities.\n\t//\n\t// Disabling this would slow down initial bootstrap process for cross\n\t// datacenter deployments. Make your own tradeoffs by configuring\n\t// --initial-election-tick-advance at the cost of slow initial bootstrap.\n\t//\n\t// If single-node, it advances ticks regardless.\n\t//\n\t// See https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/issues/9333 for more detail.\n\tInitialElectionTickAdvance bool\n\n\tBootstrapTimeout time.Duration\n\n\tAutoCompactionRetention time.Duration\n\tAutoCompactionMode      string\n\tCompactionBatchLimit    int\n\tCompactionSleepInterval time.Duration\n\tQuotaBackendBytes       int64\n\tMaxTxnOps               uint\n\n\t// MaxRequestBytes is the maximum request size to send over raft.\n\tMaxRequestBytes uint\n\n\t// MaxConcurrentStreams specifies the maximum number of concurrent\n\t// streams that each client can open at a time.\n\tMaxConcurrentStreams uint32\n\n\tWarningApplyDuration time.Duration\n\n\tStrictReconfigCheck bool\n\n\t// ClientCertAuthEnabled is true when cert has been signed by the client CA.\n\tClientCertAuthEnabled bool\n\n\tAuthToken  string\n\tBcryptCost uint\n\tTokenTTL   uint\n\n\t// InitialCorruptCheck is true to check data corruption on boot\n\t// before serving any peer/client traffic.\n\tInitialCorruptCheck     bool\n\tCorruptCheckTime        time.Duration\n\tCompactHashCheckEnabled bool\n\tCompactHashCheckTime    time.Duration\n\n\t// PreVote is true to enable Raft Pre-Vote.\n\tPreVote bool\n\n\t// SocketOpts are socket options passed to listener config.\n\tSocketOpts transport.SocketOpts","numLines":150,"startLine":1,"totalLines":348}}}
